For composers and musicians, StaffPad revolutionises the art of writing music.\r\n\r\n*IMPORTANT NOTE: STAFFPAD **REQUIRES** A DEVICE WITH ACTIVE PEN CAPABILITIES. Everything from a basic piano lead sheet to a full symphony score can be written with StaffPad.\r\n\r\nA BEAUTIFUL EXPERIENCE\r\nWriting music should be the focus of a composer. 於1999年開始研製3D虛擬毛筆。其目的是通過揮筆可造出截然不同的筆觸，而不像其他很多繪圖程式需要換‘筆刷'才得出不同的筆觸。東方用筆講求節奏，只有通過免除筆刷切換，我們才可以真正的捕捉揮筆舞動，寫出具表現力的線條。
